\DoxyCodeLine{00046\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ use\ Lloyd-\/Taylor\ model\ for\ soil\ respiration,\ in\ which\ temperature\ sensitivity\ decreases\ at\ higher\ temperatures?}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00047\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Lloyd-\/Taylor\ model\ is\ R\ =\ R0\ *\ e\string^(E0\ *\ (1/(-\/T0)\ -\/\ 1/(T\ -\/\ T0)))\ (see\ Lloyd\ and\ Taylor\ 1994,\ "{}On\ the\ temperature\ dependence\ of\ soil\ respiration"{})\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00048\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ where\ R0\ is\ rate\ at\ 0\ degrees\ C,\ T\ is\ soil\ temp.,\ E0\ and\ T0\ are\ parameters}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00499\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ Read\ climate\ file\ into\ linked\ lists,\ }}

\DoxyCodeLine{00501\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00502\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ return\ an\ array\ containing\ the\ number\ of\ time\ steps\ in\ each\ location\ (dynamically\ allocated\ with\ malloc)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00503\ \textcolor{comment}{}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00505\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ or\ a\ location\ can\ be\ skipped,\ and\ we'll\ use\ climate\ at\ location\ 0\ for\ that\ location,\ too}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00506\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00507\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ format\ of\ climFile:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00508\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ each\ line\ represents\ one\ time\ step,\ with\ the\ following\ format:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00509\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ location\ year\ day\ time\ intervalLength\ tair\ tsoil\ par\ precip\ vpd\ vpdSoil\ vPress\ wspd\ soilWetness}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00510\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ Note:\ there\ should\ be\ NO\ blank\ lines\ in\ file,\ even\ between\ different\ spatial\ locations;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00511\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ all\ entries\ for\ a\ given\ location\ should\ be\ contiguous,\ and\ locations\ should\ be\ in\ ascending\ order}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00512\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ There\ may\ be\ locations\ for\ which\ there\ is\ no\ climate\ data,\ in\ which\ case\ we\ use\ climate\ from\ location\ 0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00513\ \textcolor{comment}{*/}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00863\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ calculate\ amount\ of\ light\ absorbed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00864\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ using\ light\ attenuation\ (as\ in\ PnET)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00865\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ CURRENTLY\ UNUSED\ (see\ calcLightEff3)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00866\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ calcLightEff2\ (\textcolor{keywordtype}{double}\ *lightEff,\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{double}\ lai,\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{double}\ par)\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{00867\ \ \ \textcolor{keyword}{static}\ \textcolor{keyword}{const}\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}\ NUM\_LAYERS\ =\ 50;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00868\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00869\ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}\ layer;\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ counter}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00870\ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{double}\ cumLai\ =\ 0.0;\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ lai\ from\ this\ layer\ up}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00871\ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{double}\ lightIntensity;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00872\ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{double}\ cumLightEff\ =\ 0.0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00873\ \ \ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00874\ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}\ (lai\ >\ 0\ \&\&\ par\ >\ 0)\ \{\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ must\ have\ at\ least\ some\ leaves\ and\ some\ light}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00875\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{for}\ (layer\ =\ 1;\ layer\ <=\ NUM\_LAYERS;\ layer++)\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{00876\ \ \ \ \ \ \ cumLai\ =\ lai\ *\ ((double)layer\ /\ NUM\_LAYERS);\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ lai\ from\ this\ layer\ up}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00877\ \ \ \ \ \ \ lightIntensity\ =\ par\ *\ exp(-\/1.0\ *\ params.attenuation\ *\ cumLai);\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ between\ 0\ and\ par}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00878\ \ \ \ \ \ \ cumLightEff\ +=\ (1\ -\/\ pow(2,\ (-\/1.0\ *\ lightIntensity/params.halfSatPar)));\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ add\ between\ 0\ and\ 1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00879\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ when\ lightIntensity\ =\ halfSatPar,\ add\ 1/2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00880\ \ \ \ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00881\ \ \ \ \ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00882\ \ \ \ \ *lightEff\ =\ cumLightEff/(double)NUM\_LAYERS;\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ find\ average\ light\ effect}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00883\ \ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00884\ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ no\ leaves\ or\ no\ light!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00885\ \ \ \ \ *lightEff\ =\ 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00886\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00887\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00888\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00889\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ another\ method\ to\ calculate\ amount\ of\ light\ absorbed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00890\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ using\ light\ attenuation\ (as\ in\ PnET)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00891\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ difference\ between\ this\ and\ calcLightEff2\ is\ that\ here\ we\ use\ Simpson's\ method\ to\ approximate\ the\ integral}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00892\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ calcLightEff3\ (\textcolor{keywordtype}{double}\ *lightEff,\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{double}\ lai,\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{double}\ par)\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{00893\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00894\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ We\ are\ essentially\ integrating\ over\ the\ canopy,\ from\ top\ to\ bottom,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00895\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ but\ it's\ an\ ugly\ integral,\ so\ we'll\ approximate\ it\ numerically.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00896\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ Here\ we\ use\ Simpson's\ method\ to\ approximate\ the\ integral,\ so\ we\ need\ an\ odd\ number\ of\ points.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00897\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ This\ means\ that\ NUM\_LAYERS\ must\ be\ EVEN\ because\ we\ loop\ from\ layer\ =\ 0\ to\ layer\ =\ NUM\_LAYERS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00898\ \textcolor{comment}{\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00899\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ As\ a\ reminder,\ Simpson's\ rule\ approximates\ the\ integral\ as:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00900\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ (h/3)\ *\ (y(0)\ +\ 4y(1)\ +\ 2y(2)\ +\ 4y(3)\ +\ ...\ +\ 2y(n-\/2)\ +\ 4y(n-\/1)\ +\ y(n)),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00901\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ where\ h\ is\ the\ distance\ between\ each\ x\ value\ (here\ h\ =\ 1/NUM\_LAYERS).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00902\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ We\ keep\ track\ of\ the\ running\ sum\ in\ cumLightEff.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00903\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00904\ \ \ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00905\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Information\ on\ the\ distribution\ of\ LAI\ with\ height\ is\ available}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00906\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ as\ of\ March\ 2007\ ...\ contact\ Dr.\ Maggie\ Prater\ Maggie.Prater@colorado.edu}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00907\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00908\ \ \ \textcolor{keyword}{static}\ \textcolor{keyword}{const}\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}\ NUM\_LAYERS\ =\ 6;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00909\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ believe\ it\ or\ not,\ 6\ layers\ gives\ approximately\ the\ same\ result\ as\ 100\ layers}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00910\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00911\ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}\ layer;\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ counter}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00912\ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{double}\ cumLai;\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ lai\ from\ this\ layer\ up}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00913\ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{double}\ lightIntensity;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00914\ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{double}\ currLightEff,\ cumLightEff;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00915\ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}\ coeff;\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ current\ coefficient\ in\ Simpson's\ rule}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00916\ \ \ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00917\ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}\ (lai\ >\ 0\ \&\&\ par\ >\ 0)\ \{\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ must\ have\ at\ least\ some\ leaves\ and\ some\ light}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00918\ \ \ \ \ cumLai\ =\ 0.0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00919\ \ \ \ \ cumLightEff\ =\ 0.0;\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ the\ running\ sum}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00920\ \ \ \ \ layer\ =\ 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00921\ \ \ \ \ coeff\ =\ 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00922\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00923\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{while}\ (layer\ <=\ NUM\_LAYERS)\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{00924\ \ \ \ \ \ \ cumLai\ =\ lai\ *\ ((double)layer\ /\ NUM\_LAYERS);\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ lai\ from\ this\ layer\ up}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00925\ \ \ \ \ \ \ lightIntensity\ =\ par\ *\ exp(-\/1.0\ *\ params.attenuation\ *\ cumLai);\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ between\ 0\ and\ par}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00926\ \ \ \ \ \ \ currLightEff\ =\ (1\ -\/\ pow(2,\ (-\/1.0\ *\ lightIntensity/params.halfSatPar)));\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ between\ 0\ and\ 1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00927\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ when\ lightIntensity\ =\ halfSatPar,\ currLightEff\ =\ 1/2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00928\ \ \ \ \ \ \ cumLightEff\ +=\ coeff\ *\ currLightEff;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00929\ \ \ \ \ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00930\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ now\ move\ to\ the\ next\ layer:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00931\ \ \ \ \ \ \ layer++;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00932\ \ \ \ \ \ \ coeff\ =\ 2*(1\ +\ layer\%2);\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ coeff.\ goes\ 1,\ 4,\ 2,\ 4,\ ...,\ 2,\ 4,\ 2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00933\ \ \ \ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00934\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ last\ value\ should\ have\ had\ a\ coefficient\ of\ 1,\ but\ actually\ had\ a\ coefficient\ of\ 2,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00935\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ so\ subtract\ 1:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00936\ \ \ \ \ cumLightEff\ -\/=\ currLightEff;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00937\ \ \ \ \ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00938\ \ \ \ \ *lightEff\ =\ cumLightEff/(3.0*NUM\_LAYERS);\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ multiplying\ by\ (h/3)\ in\ Simpson's\ rule}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00939\ \ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00940\ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ no\ leaves\ or\ no\ light!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00941\ \ \ \ \ *lightEff\ =\ 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00942\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00943\ }

\DoxyCodeLine{01420\ \ \ \ \ \}}
